				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20235536' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                                                    <div class="slider_ctn">
                                        <div id="highlight_slider_left" class="slider_left"><span></span></div>
                                        <div class="slider" id="highlight_slider">
                                            <div class="slider_bg">
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="handle" style="position: absolute; left: 0px;">
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                        <div id="highlight_slider_right" class="slider_right"><span></span></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 2040;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

									<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn collapsed"><div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" id="aboutThisGame" class="game_page_autocollapse" style="max-height: 850px;">
						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							Create your own original games, import custom assets, automate games with scripting, set up complete RPG dungeons, manipulate the physics, create hinges &amp; joints, and of course flip the table when you are losing the game. All with an easy to use system integrated with Steam Workshop. You can do anything you want in Tabletop Simulator. The possibilities are endless!<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/286160/extras/TTS-Store01.jpg?t=1620412025"><h2 class="bb_tag">Endless Games</h2><br>Tabletop Simulator has it all. The base game includes 15 classics like Chess, Poker, Jigsaw Puzzles, Dominoes, and Mahjong. Additionally, there are thousands of community created content on the Workshop. If you’re the tabletop gaming type, we include an RPG Kit which has tilesets &amp; furniture, as well as animated figurines that you can set up and battle with your friends, with even more options in the Chest. There’s even an option for Game Masters so they can control the table!<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/286160/extras/TTS-Store08.jpg?t=1620412025"><h2 class="bb_tag">Create Games</h2><br>If you’re into creativity and prototyping, you can easily create your own games by importing images onto custom boards &amp; tables, create custom decks, import 3D models, create scripts, and much more. You can choose to upload your creations on the Steam Workshop or share them privately with your friends.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/286160/extras/TTS-Store02.jpg?t=1620412025"><h2 class="bb_tag">Fun For All Ages</h2><br>Everyone can play Tabletop Simulator! Play a classic board game with grandma, have poker night with the guys, or start your epic RPG adventure with your crew. Play almost any tabletop game you can think of! Being a multiplayer-focused game, up to <strong>10</strong> players can play at any given time. <br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/286160/extras/TTS-Store05.jpg?t=1620412025"><h2 class="bb_tag">DLCs</h2><br>Our downloadable content (DLCs) are different from other games, as we partner with developers and publishers to bring their games into Tabletop Simulator. Each DLC is custom created with  high quality assets and  special themes that match their games. And best of all, only the host needs to own the DLC for everyone at the table to play.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/286160/extras/TTS-Store07.jpg?t=1620412025"><br><br><strong>Key Features</strong>:<br><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Online sandbox with unlimited games to play how you want.<br></li><li>Multiplayer physics with objects that collide and interact just how you would expect. <br></li><li>Create your own mods easily with full Steam Workshop support and 3D model importing. <br></li><li>Take games to the next level with Lua scripting support.<br></li><li>Play just like you do in real life; pick up, rotate, shake, and throw any object.<br></li><li>Up to 10 people can play together on the same table.<br></li><li>Team system with voice and text chat.<br></li><li>Save &amp; load individual objects and complete games.<br></li><li>Hotseat allows you to play locally on the same computer with your friends.<br></li><li>Browse the internet, listen to music, and watch videos in multiplayer, in-game on a tablet. <br></li><li>Perfect for RPGs - build your very own roleplaying dungeons with our modular tileset, RPG Kit, Multiple States and Tablet (useful for character sheets). <br></li><li>Great admin tools to enable or disable player permissions and to eliminate griefing in public games. <br></li><li>360° panoramic backgrounds that change the lighting and atmosphere. <br></li><li>Included games: Backgammon, Cards, Chess, Checkers, Chinese Checkers, Custom Board, Dice, Dominoes, Go, Jigsaw Puzzles, Mahjong, Pachisi, Piecepack, Poker, Reversi, RPG Kit, Sandbox, Solitaire, and Tablet.</li></ul>						</div>

		$J( function() {

			var $Content = $J('.sysreq_content');

			$Tabs.click( function() {
				var $Tab = $J(this);
				$Tabs.removeClass('active');
				$Tab.addClass('active');

				$Content.removeClass('active');
				$Content.filter('[data-os=' + $Tab.data('os') + ']').addClass('active');

				$Content.trigger('gamepage_autocollapse_expand');
			});

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary136215560_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：4 月 7 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					说服朋友买这个东西(x)<br>趁着打折干脆先斩后奏给好友买了，直接开一盘紧张刺激的桌游(√)<br><br>从万智牌过来的。约莫一年前的时候，我无法抑制住自己想和喜欢的男生来往的热情，于是给他（我的高中同学）和我的其他舍友买了一个4人包。那时我上大一。<br>八月份告了白，失败了，对方是直男。<br>桌游模拟器承载着我一年前的爱意与苦楚。如今我打开这游戏，与其说是在看桌游，不如说是在翻老照片。真是让人怀念啊。<br>现在还能隔三岔五和这位高中同学一起搓两把桌游真是太好了……（落泪）我俩一个在东北一个在南昌，要是实体打牌。恐怕得等到牌堆发霉了。<br><br>小故事先到这。<br>只要你不缺朋友，这游戏一定是你们的派对首选！<br>小到骇狼求生，万智，Uno，大到幽港迷城，诡境奇谭，甚至DND……TTS的模组和引擎配合上创意工坊有志人士的辛苦迁移，可以说是完成了绝大部分桌游从实体到电脑上的移植。<br>桌游实体版是昂贵的，亲朋好友是难聚的。如果对桌游感兴趣却找不到朋友可玩，或是手头正紧掏不出买桌游的钱，随时欢迎加入桌游模拟器的社群。<br>TTS最大程度还原了玩家游玩桌游时的体验，即便仍有许多可以优化的地方（比如网络 嗯），游戏本身加上创意工坊的内容也已足够充实。<br><br>买吧买吧买吧 有伴儿你不买那真的太亏了 真的好玩儿的！<br><br>关于购买与折扣信息：<br>本体很少打折，一般在季节特惠时偶尔会折一下。阿区比国区便宜许多，如有阿区的话可以考虑。<br>DLC不推荐买！DLC有的创意工坊也有，DLC没有的创意工坊还有。怎么看都是不买划算。<br><br>朋友多些当然还是买四人包更便宜啊。<br><br>不知道玩什么桌游可以去国内的桌游社区“集石”那里去看，规则书一般也能从那里找到。在此感谢诸位汉化工作者的辛勤耕作！没有你们的转译，咱这笨蛋英文水平看规则书的目录都觉得吃力啊——<br><br>安装的注意事项：<br>安装桌游模拟器后先别打开，去创意工坊安装简体中文翻译（一般搜Simplified Chinese或简中就会有），否则你会被官方的直译整成呜呜伯。<br>订阅了先别急，打开桌游模拟器后点一下右下角那个红蓝相间的方块。从那里可以调整语言。<br><br>可以完成新手教程（toterials,在“开始菜单中间的小按钮里”）来了解其中的基本操作，Esc——帮助这里也能看到游戏的键位和对应功能。<br><br>联机记得把掀桌关了:)<br><br>关于模组：<br>创意工坊中的mod包有的要挂梯子才能完全载入，而有的mod则因作者挂的链接太久未更新失效了，可能是无法载入的。<br>这时可以将模组包下载到本地，可以试着到网上搜索，也有人做出了整理。如：<a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://docs.qq.com/sheet/DRHNteENuaU5VdGRs?scode=&amp;tab=BB08J2" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://docs.qq.com/sheet/DRHNteENuaU5VdGRs?scode=&amp;tab=BB08J2</a><br><a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://www.imdodo.com/channel/127803/476330" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://www.imdodo.com/channel/127803/476330</a><br>将模组下载到本地进行联机游戏时，需要每个玩家都将资源下载至本地方能正常加载；而创意工坊则只需创建房间的人订阅。<br><br>创意工坊中也有带汉化的模组，有好人将其整理成了合集。汉化过了的模组一般也是能够加载出来的，如果不能，可以到留言那里提醒作者。<br><br><br><br>2023.9.2，修改联机部分的内容：<br><br>你可以放弃所有的局域网软件去选择ZeroTier！主机去那里注册账号后创建服务器<br><a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://my.zerotier.com/network/" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://my.zerotier.com/network/</a><br>而后叫其他客机好友下载相应的软件（你可以去官方网站下，但大概率下不上。<br>链接：<a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://pan.ba" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://pan.ba</a> <a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=http://idu.com/s/1dYqNVhyn" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">idu.com/s/1dYqNVhyn</a> cPTVJTtqKQ uKJw?pwd=Zer0  提取码：Zer0，直接发链接会被吞），连上你的服务器ID。<br>想检验下连接效果的话，可以从终端那边ping一下那上面写的虚拟IP地址。目前来看这是联机效果最好，也是最稳定的方案。人数上没问题——50人之内都是没问题的。<br><br>下面是一些可能失效了或者价格上不太亲民的联机方案……？<br>加速器连同一节点：据我打牌的朋友说，裸连还真行！steam++这样的就够了。<br><br>另一种方式是建立本地的局域网，听说的有三样。<br>1.蒲公英访问端：免费提供三个成员位置，若需额外购置成员位置则需要购置会员端。会员端每个人都要付费，价格是88人/年。（意味着如果你要四个人联机，要至少一年支付352r/人/年。）<br>你真的好贵……<br><br>2.游侠平台：——这个更贵。季卡36，年卡132，还是新人优惠。怎么看都不算划算的选择……但也可以试试。<br>打算长时间组网的话，其实蒲公英的水平就够了。<br><br>3.Radmin LAN：我很少遇到用这个软件也可以联机的情况。先前我说的距离近了可以联机……那种情况下裸连其实也差不了太多。这个还是不推荐了。<br><br>最近创意工坊更新了脚本化的王权骰铸，好玩。玩一下。<br>墨镜大佬做了以撒的结合四魂：镇魂曲汉化的工作，同时正在为之前秋落大大翻译的卡牌做勘误，自己还翻译了官方的规则书。<br>想再玩玩四魂的话可以去他的创意工坊！搜墨镜哥就行，没问题的。<br><br><br>……可惜笔者的朋友一个个又忙起来啦。忙着打派，忙着交女朋友，忙这忙那……好，忙点好啊。<br>祝你们能遇到可以打一辈子桌游的朋友。<br><br>考虑到稳定的联机方案已经找到了，这篇评测短时间内应该不会再更新。希望这些能帮到你们。					<div class="gradient"></div>

					<div class="bb_h1">最难的一步：说服朋友买这个东西</div><br>总评<br>+桌游模拟器 创意工坊无限桌游<br>+设置简单 不需要整理收纳太减负<br>+工坊汉化 官中机翻痕迹严重，建议使用zsy314大佬的工坊翻译<br><br>±需要朋友 能通过其他途径语音的那种<br><br>-操作略难懂 请认真完成新手教程，并稍微需要熟练一下<br>-考验网速 现实距离太远有掉线风险，另外建议提前下载好对应工坊的图包否则可能会加载不出来orz<br><br>关于游戏<br>需要朋友！需要朋友！需要朋友！<br>重要的事情说三遍。如果没有可以开黑的人选，不建议购买。当然，如果想体验孤独感请随意。<br>满足条件的桌游爱好者必备。<br>请给我一个不买它的理由（手动doge<br><br>关于中文<br>进入创意工坊后，搜索物品限制种类“Translation”，即可轻松找到简中翻译模组，直接订阅即可。<br>启动游戏后，点击主页面右下角语言选择，左列选择中文，右列选择该项目。<br>最后再次感谢zsy314大佬提供的汉化，让我可以顺利完成新手教程！					<div class="gradient"></div>
